<a name="s.11"></a>
\par \textbf{S.11 Files}

\begin{tabularx}
<td valign=top>File^{\ }_{\ } & \ & <td valign=top>\textbf{\Phi}_{\textit{\ j}}^{\textit{\ i}} & \ & A representation of \mathbf{a} of the form\\ (\mathbf{p}_{1}, \mathbf{a}_{1}, \mathbf{p}_{2}, \mathbf{a}_{2}, ..., \mathbf{a}_{\textit{\nu}(\mathbf{a})}, \mathbf{p}_{\textit{\nu}(\mathbf{a})+1}, ∘, \mathbf{p}_{\textit{\nu}(\mathbf{a})+2}, ..., \mathbf{p}_{\textit{\nu}(\mathbf{p})}), where \mathbf{p}_{\textit{h}} is the partition at position \textit{h}, \mathbf{p}_{1} = \mathbf{p}_{\textit{\nu}(\mathbf{p})} = \textit{\lambda}, and (\textbf{⍺}^{1} \wedge \textbf{⍵}^{1})/\mathbf{p} \subseteq \textbf{\lambda}. & <td valign=top align=right><a href="#file_defn"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td nowrap valign=top>Position file^{\ }_{\ } & \ & <td valign=top>\textit{\pi}(\textbf{\Phi}_{\textit{\ j}}^{\textit{\ i}}) ← \textit{h} & \ & Set file to position \textit{h}. Called \textit{rewind} if \textit{h} = 1, and \textit{wind} if \textit{h} = \textit{\nu}(\mathbf{p}). & <td valign=top align=right><a href="#file_position"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td colspan=6>Record (from position \textit{h}) & \\
<td valign=top>\ \ Forward^{\ }_{\ } & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>_{0}\textbf{\Phi}_{\textit{\ j}}^{\textit{\ i}} ← \mathbf{a}, \textbf{\lambda}_{\textit{k}} & \ & \mathbf{a}_{\textit{h}} ← \mathbf{a}, \mathbf{p}_{\textit{h}+1} ← \textbf{\lambda}_{\textit{k}}; stop at position \textit{h} + 1. Zero prescript may be elided and \textbf{\lambda}_{1} may be elided. & <td valign=top align=right><a href="#forward_record"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\ \\
<td valign=top nowrap>\ \ Backward^{\ }_{\ } & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>_{1}\textbf{\Phi}_{\textit{\ j}}^{\textit{\ i}} ← \mathbf{a}, \textbf{\lambda}_{\textit{k}} & \ & \mathbf{a}_{\textit{h}-1} ← \mathbf{a}, \mathbf{p}_{\textit{h}-1} ← \textbf{\lambda}_{\textit{k}}; stop at position \textit{h} - 1. \textbf{\lambda}_{1} may be elided. & <td valign=top align=right><a href="#backward_record"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td colspan=6>Read (from position \textit{h}) & \\
<td valign=top>\ \ Forward^{\ }_{\ } & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textit{a}, \textit{b} ← _{0}\textbf{\Phi}_{\textit{\ j}}^{\textit{\ i}} & \ & \textit{a} ← \mathbf{a}_{\textit{h}}; \textit{b} ← \mathbf{p}_{\textit{h}+1}; stop at position \textit{h} + 1. Associated branch is controlled by \mathbf{p}_{\textit{h}+1}, and \textit{b} may be elided. Zero prescript may be elided. & <td valign=top align=right><a href="#forward_read"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>\ \ Backward^{\ }_{\ } & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textit{a}, \textit{b} ← _{1}\textbf{\Phi}_{\textit{\ j}}^{\textit{\ i}} & \ & \textit{a} ← \mathbf{a}_{\textit{h}-1}; \textit{b} ← \mathbf{p}_{\textit{h}-1}; stop at position \textit{h} - 1. Associated branch is controlled by \mathbf{p}_{\textit{h}-1} and \textit{b} may be elided. & <td valign=top align=right><a href="#backward_read"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td colspan=6>File array & \\
<td valign=top>\ \ Full^{\ }_{\ } & \ & <td valign=top>\textbf{\Phi}^{\ }_{\ } & \ & Array of files \textbf{\Phi}_{\textit{\ j}}^{\textit{\ i}}, for \textit{i} ∊ \textbf{⍳}^{1}(\textit{\mu}(\textbf{\Phi})), \textit{j} ∊ \textbf{⍳}^{1}(\textit{\nu}(\textbf{\Phi})). & <td valign=top align=right><a href="#file_array"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>\ \ Row^{\ }_{\ } & \ & <td valign=top>\textbf{\Phi}^{\textit{\ i}}_{\ } & \ & Row of files \textbf{\Phi}_{\textit{\ j}}^{\textit{\ i}}, for \textit{j} ∊ \textbf{⍳}^{1}(\textit{\nu}(\textbf{\Phi})). & <td valign=top align=right><a href="#file_array"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\

\begin{tabularx}
<td valign=top nowrap>Path \mathbf{i}_{\ }^{\ }} & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\mathbf{c} ← \textbf{A}^{\mathbf{i}} & \ & <td valign=top>\mathbf{c}_{1} is the \mathbf{i}_{1}th root of \textbf{A}; \mathbf{c}_{\textit{\ j}} is the \mathbf{i}_{\textit{\ j\ }}th node of the nodes on level \textit{j} reachable from node \mathbf{c}_{\textit{\ j}-1}. & <td valign=top align=right>^{\ }_{\ }<a href="#path"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\

<td valign=top>Component-by-\\component} & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{C} ← \textbf{A} <img src="APLimg/circledot.bmp"> \textbf{B}^{\ } & \ & <td valign=top>(\textbf{C}^{\ \mathbf{i}})_{\textit{\nu}(\mathbf{i})} = (\textbf{A}^{\ \mathbf{i}})_{\textit{\nu}(\mathbf{i})} <img src="APLimg/circledot.bmp"> (\textbf{B}^{\ \mathbf{i}})_{\textit{\nu}(\mathbf{i})}. & <td valign=top align=right>^{\ }_{\ }<a href="#1.23.7"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>Path reduction} & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{C} ← <img src="APLimg/circledot.bmp">/\textbf{A} & \ & <td valign=top>Reduction by operator or relation <img src="APLimg/circledot.bmp"> on nodes in left list order. & <td valign=top align=right>^{\ }_{\ }<a href="#tree_reduction"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\

<td valign=top nowrap>\textit{j}-origin \mathbf{b}-index}_{\ } & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{B} ← \mathbf{b} \textbf{⍳}_{\textit{j}} \textbf{A} & \ & <td valign=top>(\textbf{B}^{\ \mathbf{i}})_{\textit{\nu}(\mathbf{i})} = \mathbf{b} \textbf{⍳}_{\textit{j}} ((\textbf{A}^{\mathbf{i}})_{\textit{\nu}(\mathbf{i})}) & <td valign=top align=right>^{\ }_{\ }<a href="#tree_iota"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top nowrap>\textit{j}-origin mapping_{\ } & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{C} ← \mathbf{b} \int_{\textit{j}} \textbf{A} & \ & <td valign=top>Rooted subtree \textbf{C}_{\textit{i}} is a single null character node if \mathbf{b}_{\textit{i}} \notin \textbf{⍺}^{\textit{j}}(\textbf{\mu}_{1}(\textbf{A})); otherwise \textbf{C}_{i} = \textbf{A}_{\mathbf{b}_{\textit{i}}}, where \textbf{A} is treated in a \textit{j}-origin system. & <td valign=top align=right>^{\ }_{\ }<a href="#tree_map"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>Full right list\\matrix & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\mathbf{C} ← ]\textbf{A} & <td rowspan=2><img align=left src="APLimg/matrixr4.bmp"> & <td valign=top rowspan=2>The rows of the index matrix <img src="APLimg/alphaboscore.bmp">^{2}/\mathbf{C} are the right (left) justified index vectors (with null fill to the common dimension \textit{\nu}(\textbf{A})) arranged in increasing order; \mathbf{C}_{1} and \mathbf{C}_{2} are the corresponding degree and node vectors of \textbf{A}. & <td valign=top align=right rowspan=2>^{\ }_{\ }<a href="#1.23.3"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>Full left list\\matrix & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\mathbf{C} ← [\textbf{A} & \\
<td valign=top>Right list matrix & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\mathbf{C} ← \textbf{⍺}^{2}/]\textbf{A} & <td rowspan=2><img align=left src="APLimg/matrixr2.bmp"> & <td valign=top rowspan=2>The degree and node vector columns of the full right (left) list. & <td valign=top align=right rowspan=2><a href="#1.23.3"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>Left list matrix & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\mathbf{C} ← \textbf{⍺}^{2}/[\textbf{A} & \\
<td valign=top>Tree compression & \ & <td valign=top>\textbf{C} ← \textbf{U}/\textbf{A} & \ & \textbf{C} is obtained from \textbf{A} by suppressing node \mathbf{i} if node \mathbf{i} of \textbf{U} is zero and reconnecting so that for each remaining pair of nodes, the one lies in the subtree rooted at the second if and only if it did so in \textbf{A}. & <td valign=top align=right><a href="#1.23.6"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>Path compression & \ & <td valign=top>\textbf{C} ← \mathbf{u}/\textbf{A} & \ & \textbf{C} is obtained from \textbf{A} by suppressing all nodes on level \textit{j} if \mathbf{u}_{\textit{j}} = 0, and reconnecting as in the compression \textbf{U}/\textbf{A}. & <td valign=top align=right><a href="#path_compression"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>Level compression & \ & <td valign=top>\textbf{C} ← \mathbf{u}//\textbf{A} & \ & \textbf{C} is obtained from \textbf{A} by suppressing rooted subtree \textbf{A}_{\textit{j}} if \mathbf{u}_{\textit{j}} = 0. & <td valign=top align=right>^{\ }<a href="#level_compression"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>Level mesh & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{C} ← \\\textbf{A}, \mathbf{u}, \textbf{B}\\ & \ & <img src="APLimg/uboscore.bmp">//\textbf{C} = \textbf{A}; \mathbf{u}//\textbf{C} = \textbf{B}. & \\
<td valign=top>Level mask & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{C} ← //\textbf{A}, \mathbf{u}, \textbf{B}// & \ & <img src="APLimg/uboscore.bmp">//\textbf{C} = <img src="APLimg/uboscore.bmp">//\textbf{A}; \mathbf{u}//\textbf{C} = \mathbf{u}//\textbf{B}. & \\
<td valign=top>Path catenation & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{C} ← \textbf{A} <img src="APLimg/circleplus.bmp"> \textbf{B} & \ & \textbf{C} is obtained by connecting roots of \textbf{B} to leaves of \textbf{A}, allotting successive groups of at most ⌈\textbf{\mu}_{1}(\textbf{B}) ÷ \textit{\lambda}(\textbf{A})⌉ roots of \textbf{B} to each successive leaf of \textbf{A}. & <td valign=top align=right><a href="#1.23"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>Full tree & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{W} ← <font face="Arial">\textbf{E}</font> & \ & Each node of \textbf{W} is unity and the structure of \textbf{W} is determined by compatibility. & <td valign=top align=right><a href="#full_tree"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>\ & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{W} ← <font face="Arial">\textbf{E}</font>(\mathbf{k}) & \ & Each node of \textbf{W} is unity; \textbf{W} is homogeneous (i.e., all nodes on any level have a common degree) and \textbf{\nu}(\textbf{W}) = \mathbf{k}. & <td valign=top align=right><a href="#full_tree_k"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>Zero tree & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{W} ← <img src="APLimg/0tree.bmp">\\ \textbf{W} ← 0 & <img src="APLimg/bracketsx12.bmp"> & Each node of \textbf{W} is zero and the structure of \textbf{W} is determined by compatibility. & <td valign=top align=right><a href="#full_tree"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>\ & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{W} ← <img src="APLimg/0tree.bmp">(\mathbf{k})</font> & \ & Each node of \textbf{W} is zero; \textbf{W} is homogeneous and \textbf{\nu}(\textbf{W}) = \mathbf{k}. & <td valign=top align=right><a href="#full_tree_k"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>Path tree^{\ } & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{W} ← ^{\mathbf{u}}<font face="Arial">\textbf{E}</font> & \ & <img src="APLimg/uboscore.bmp">/\textbf{W} = 0; \mathbf{u}/\textbf{W} = <font face="Arial">\textbf{E}</font>; structure of \textbf{W} determined by compatibility. & <td valign=top align=right><a href="#full_tree"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>\ & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{W} ← ^{\mathbf{u}}<font face="Arial">\textbf{E}</font>(\mathbf{k}) & \ & <img src="APLimg/uboscore.bmp">/\textbf{W} = 0; \mathbf{u}/\textbf{W} = <font face="Arial">\textbf{E}</font>; \textbf{W} is homogeneous and \textbf{\nu}(\textbf{W}) = \mathbf{k}. & <td valign=top align=right><a href="#full_tree_k"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>Level tree_{\ } & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{W} ← _{\mathbf{u}}<font face="Arial">\textbf{E}</font> & \ & <img src="APLimg/uboscore.bmp">//\textbf{W} = 0; \mathbf{u}//\textbf{W} = <font face="Arial">\textbf{E}</font>; structure of \textbf{W} determined by compatibility. & <td valign=top align=right><a href="#full_tree"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>\ & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{W} ← _{\mathbf{u}}<font face="Arial">\textbf{E}</font>(\mathbf{k}) & \ & <img src="APLimg/uboscore.bmp">//\textbf{W} = 0; \mathbf{u}//\textbf{W} = <font face="Arial">\textbf{E}</font>; \textbf{W} is homogeneous and \textbf{\nu}(\textbf{W}) = \mathbf{k}. & <td valign=top align=right><a href="#full_tree_k"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>Maximization & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{W} ← \textbf{U} ⌈ \textbf{A} & <td rowspan=2><img src="APLimg/matrixr2.bmp"> & <td rowspan=2>\textbf{W} = \textbf{U} \wedge (\textbf{A} = \textit{m}<font face="Arial">\textbf{E}</font>), where \textit{m} is the maximum (minimum) over all nodes of \textbf{U}/\textbf{A}. & <td valign=top align=right><a href="#tree_max"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>Minimization & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{W} ← \textbf{U} ⌊ \textbf{A} & \\
<td valign=top>Maximum path prefix & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{W} ← ⍺/\textbf{U}</font> & \ & \textbf{W} is obtained from \textbf{U} by zeroing all nodes of every subtree rooted in a zero node. & <td valign=top align=right><a href="#fig1.24"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>Maximum path suffix & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{W} ← ⍵/\textbf{U}</font> & \ & \textbf{W} is obtained from \textbf{U} by zeroing every node which contains a zero node in its subtree. & <td valign=top align=right><a href="#fig1.24"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>Forward path set selector & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{W} ← \textit{\sigma}/\textbf{A}</font> & \ & (\textbf{W}^{\ \mathbf{i}})_{\textit{\nu}(\mathbf{i})} = 1 if (\textbf{A}^{\mathbf{i}})_{\textit{\nu}(\mathbf{i})} differs from all preceding nodes of path \textbf{A}^{\mathbf{i}}. & <td valign=top align=right>^{\ }<a href="#fig1.24"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>Backward path set selector & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{W} ← \textit{\tau}/\textbf{A}</font> & \ & (\textbf{W}^{\ \mathbf{i}})_{\textit{\nu}(\mathbf{i})} = 1 if (\textbf{A}^{\mathbf{i}})_{\textit{\nu}(\mathbf{i})} differs from all other nodes in its subtree. & <td valign=top align=right>^{\ }<a href="#fig1.24"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>Maximum level^{\ } prefix & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{W} ← ⍺//\textbf{U}</font> ^{\ } & \ & <td valign=top>\textbf{∊}^{\textit{\ j}}/\textbf{W} = ⍺/\textbf{∊}^{\textit{\ j}}/\textbf{U} & <td valign=top align=right>^{\ }<a href="#fig1.24"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>Maximum level^{\ } suffix & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{W} ← ⍵//\textbf{U}</font> ^{\ } & \ & <td valign=top>\textbf{∊}^{\textit{\ j}}/\textbf{W} = ⍵/\textbf{∊}^{\textit{\ j}}/\textbf{U} & <td valign=top align=right>^{\ }<a href="#fig1.24"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>Forward level^{\ }\\ set selector & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{W} ← \textit{\sigma}//\textbf{A}</font> ^{\ } & \ & <td valign=top>\textbf{∊}^{\textit{\ j}}/\textbf{W} = \textit{\sigma}/\textbf{∊}^{\textit{\ j}}/\textbf{U} & <td valign=top align=right>^{\ }<a href="#fig1.24"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
<td valign=top>Backward level^{\ } set selector & \ & <td valign=top nowrap>\textbf{W} ← \textit{\tau}//\textbf{A}</font> ^{\ } & \ & <td valign=top>\textbf{∊}^{\textit{\ j}}/\textbf{W} = \textit{\tau}/\textbf{∊}^{\textit{\ j}}/\textbf{U} & <td valign=top align=right>^{\ }<a href="#fig1.24"><img src="APLimg/link.bmp"></a> & \\
\end{tabularx}
